msg:Traveling back to Shanghai with my wife by car, just passing by Nanjing, thinking of going to Tangshan for a hot spring trip to wash the soul the next day, so I booked this hotel, the hotel is listed with five stars, the location is relatively easy to find, just at the intersection, not far away It is the commercial street, a few kilometers away there are some scenic spots and Bailian Outlets. I just wandered around Nanjing first, then went to Ole to buy something, and went to the hotel at 3.4 o'clock in the afternoon. The subway is currently under construction in front of the hotel, and a large block is enclosed. Watching the construction, the car was parked in the underground garage, and the registration of the license plate at the front desk of the residents was free.
Check-in and check-out at the front desk are very efficient. Thinking of taking a private bath, I specially booked a hot spring room. The only downside is that the room is really small, but I think that there is a pool in the balcony, and the hot spring water can be directly introduced. It is still very good, and I want to soak Just soak, there is also an electric curtain on the balcony, which is also very private. Remind that there are more mosquitoes in the season, and the sliding doors of rooms and balconies must be closed, but the hotel is also equipped with electric mosquito coils for use.
The hotel‚Äôs breakfast is from 7:00 to 10:00. On the first floor of the main building, there are signs, just go through the children‚Äôs paradise. The breakfast is pretty good, at least better than the five-star hotel in the city where I stayed the day before. You can make your own waffles, and you can also try the old duck vermicelli soup. The restaurant reception and service staff are also very enthusiastic. You can choose a position by the window while eating breakfast while admiring the garden-like landscape outside the window. After eating, you can walk around in the courtyard, or you can go upstairs to rest for a while and continue to soak before checking out.
There is also a hot spring open to the public on the roof of the north building of the hotel. I went and visited it. There are several hot springs and trees, and the scenery is also good. If you don't have a room with hot spring hot springs, I recommend you to try it. The fare is also concessionary for residents, and it seems to be 80 yuan per person. There is a small gym and swimming pool on the 6th floor of the main building, which may be less crowded in the off-season.
If you want to have dinner on the day of check-in, there is also a Chinese set menu in the hotel, and the price is not very expensive. I chose to walk to the side and explore it. I walked out of the parking lot gate on the left hand side, and walked across a street in the direction of the Workers‚Äô Nursing Home and Chiang Kai-shek Hot Spring Villa. There are milk tea fried chicken spots and everything else. I saw a lot of food stalls in the big yard of a car repair shop next to me. I haven't eaten a food stall for a long time, so I went in and had a meal. The big lobster for 100 yuan and 4 catties was still very cool.
The overall hotel facilities are pretty good, much better than the old five-star I live in the city. Recently, summer is the off-season of hot springs, and there are indeed not many people. It is deserted and of course it just happened to be off the peak for me. You can consider bringing your family with you in the next meeting. The suggestion is to ask the hotel to consider putting a shelf that can be dried on the balcony; I have my birthday a few days ago, and it is also the off-season anyway, I can really consider upgrading my room for free ü§≠
